=== 特訓完整字庫 ===

1. [art.] a --> 一個 || I have a dog. （我有一隻狗。）
2. [adv.] a.m. --> 上午 || The meeting starts at 9:00 a.m. （會議在上午九點開始。）
3. [v.] abandon --> 放棄 || They had to abandon the car. （他們不得不放棄那輛車。）
4. [v.] abbreviate --> 縮寫 || "Doctor" is abbreviated to "Dr." （"Doctor"被縮寫為"Dr."。）
5. [v.] abide --> 遵守 || You must abide by the rules. （你必須遵守規則。）
6. [n.] ability --> 能力 || She has the ability to succeed. （她有成功的能力。）
7. [adj.] able --> 有能力的 || He is able to speak three languages. （他能說三種語言。）
8. [adj.] abnormal --> 異常 || The test results were abnormal. （測試結果是異常的。）
9. [prep./adv.] aboard --> 船上 || All passengers aboard the plane were safe. （飛機上的所有乘客都是安全的。）
10. [v.] abolish --> 取消 || The government decided to abolish the tax. （政府決定取消這項稅收。）
11. [adj./n.] aboriginal --> 原住民 || We visited an aboriginal village. （我們參觀了一個原住民的村莊。）
12. [n.] abortion --> 流產 || She had to undergo an abortion. （她不得不接受人工流產。）
13. [v.] abound --> 盛產 || The lake abounds with fish. （這個湖泊盛產魚類。）
14. [prep./adv.] about --> 關於 || What is this book about? （這本書是關於什麼的？）
15. [prep./adv./adj.] above --> 在上方 || The sun rose above the horizon. （太陽升到了地平線上方。）
16. [adv.] abroad --> 在國外 || She loves to travel abroad. （她喜歡到國外旅遊。）
17. [adj.] abrupt --> 突然的 || The road made an abrupt turn to the left. （道路突然向左轉彎。）
18. [n.] absence --> 缺席 || Her absence from the meeting was noticed. （她在會議上的缺席被注意到了。）
19. [adj./v.] absent --> 缺席的 || He was absent from class today. （他今天上課缺席。）
